<rate>2</rate>< review>
Still looking for an honest automotive shop. Over all, I wouldn't recommend this store. Angel was the writer I talked to (who was nice, buddy buddy like). I explained what my car was doing and he gave me his thoughts. I told him what I thought it was based upon previous service by another dealer and myself. After leaving it at the shop, he called me a day or two later and gave me a whopping $1,900 estimate. He guaranteed me this should fix my issue. As upset with the ticket amount, I didn't listen as closely as I should have to everything they where doing to the car...just sold/blinded on the fact they found my issue and was going to fix it. Turns out, I got a water pump and hose that was leaking, trans service that I didn't need, an oil change I didn't request and they changed my engine and trans mounts that I DID need. They said my water pump was leaking and when I mentioned that was my oil leak, they said it was the water pump. Funny...I've never needed to fill my coolant. Angel was nice, but he's responsible for his mechanics honesty. Tho my shifting issues seemed less noticeable with new mounts, my problem reappeared by the time I got straight home from their shop. I called Angel and informed him immediately. He said he'd make it right. After waiting, I called corporate to see if I could get a second opinion at a different store, instead they sent me to the owner of this shop, Larry. He was nice, wanted to make it better and briefly tried to fix one of many oil leaks they said I didn't have, which didn't make a difference of course. They said they would call me in a couple months to straighten out the rest of  the work, but never heard back. Their shop is IMMACULATE (and impressed me), but they are not careful with your car. They splashed coolant on both sides of my fenders and a small nick of paint off one of them (see lower left in pic). I don't wish to return, I'll be taking all FIVE of my cars somewhere else. I would recommend you going elsewhere and get another opinion.< /review>

< review>
The only reason I gave this place two stars is because I like my actual apartment and the location of the building, and the housekeeping staff keep up well with the slobs that live here. Other than that, it's a free-for-all with parking even though they have assigned spots. Anybody and everybody can get into the parking garage and the guest spots are taken by people who never move. Twice I have found someone parked in my spot (tandem parking is reserved)-and forget asking the "courtesy patrol quote to do anything about it-they won't tow the vehicles. They put a "warning" on the vehicle and it just sits there until it's moved. My experience with the above named patrol, who never did put a warning on the vehicle in my spot, was incredibly unhelpful. I pay rent for this? Do yourself a favor and find a more secure building.

<review>I had set an appointment for an AUTO BUTLER on 2/5/20 @ 9:00 a.m.  I was greeted nicely and after a few minutes was greeted once again, this time by Guillermo (Gil) Portillo, Service Advisor.  After looking over my car and taking down some notes on his pad, we entered the Service Department.  Gil asked me if I needed transportation anywhere...I told him no, that I was going to have to wait until the car was finished.  He advised me that the coating would take a minimum of 4 hours, and that there was a car in front of me. <Rate>5<//Rate>< Review>
I had set an appointment for an AUTO BUTLER on 2/5/20 @ 9:00 a.m.  I was greeted nicely and after a few minutes was greeted once again, this time by Guillermo (Gil) Portillo, Service Advisor.  After looking over my car and taking down some notes on his pad, we entered the Service Department.  Gil asked me if I needed transportation anywhere...I told him no, that I was going to have to wait until the car was finished.  He advised me that the coating would take a minimum of 4 hours, and that there was a car in front of me.  I told him that I was there "for the duration" and needed to wait for my vehicle until finished.  While I listened to my I POD, Gil came around and said to me if I would like to go home now?  I looked at my watch, and it was 10:54 a.m.  THAT really surprised me.  I guess Gil took pity on me, said he talked to "his guys" and they promised to get on the job quickly so I wouldn't have to wait that long....and folks, there you are.  Another great visit to Capitol Buick GMC, and I now consider Gil mi amigo, and know that he's really there to help me out.  Thank you very much, Gil!!!!!!!<//Review>

The yogurt mill is definitely the best place to go get frozen yogurt. On summer nights you can easily wait up to 30 minutes trying to get a yogurt. The line is visible from the street. If that doesn't tell you how good the yogurt is wait until you see the sizes. You can drop any of the smaller sizes into the next size up for 10 cents! Try their yogurt. It really is good. < Review>
Husband and I were visiting family in the area from AZ... Husband use to go here when he was a kid and said it was "awesome".
When we arrived we were rushed into ordering without being able to try any samples. We ordered the "child" size which is about a 4 cup serving. I hastily ordered coffee, my husband thin mint. To our dismay, the yogurt was not good quality, and the coffee had a horrible aftertaste. Because I work in the Customer Service industry I did not want to be "that customer", so I had my husband purchase me a new yogurt in the smallest size and pay for it. When we were attempting to leave, I asked the attendants if they had a place in back that would be more suitable to throw away the ridiculous amount of coffee yogurt instead of their outdoor trashcans. The attendant made it a point that she would like to give our money back because I shouldn't have payed for a replacement. When she consulted her more senior coworker on the subject, she proceeded to loudly explain that because we ordered a different size and did not ask them to begin with, they could not refund my money. After hearing her explain this three times, I was finally able to get a word in. "I do not want my money back, all I want is for you to throw this away for me." I left, and as my husband was leaving both workers apologized and said they hope that we would return. He explained "we won't, we're from AZ and we will never stop here again".</Review>

This place has been around forever...and for a reason:  it is absolutely wonderful frozen yogurt. < Text>
When I think of a great place to have a cold treat, I always think of the Yogurt Mill. They always have great flavors (but they change daily so call ahead or check their Instagram). My favorite flavor is Oreos and Cream, which is offered every Thursday. This frozen Yogurt shop offers really big portions, and has lots of "buy one get one free" coupons all the time.  Make sure to bring one for you, and print an extra for a friend/neighbor.  Bring your cash.  This shop is CASH ONLY, but totally worth it.</Text>

< Review>
I've been here twice and I'm never coming back here. Let's see, where to start:

They don't seem to offer individual sizes; in my opinion they have: baby size cup and the other cups they offer are better fit for extremely large people. The only reason I came back once was because there's always a long line that catches my attention; it makes you think it's a place worth going to, but as soon as I stepped into the business, I remember why I hate it: slow workers (who don't even offer napkins?), not enough chairs/space, not interesting atmosphere (gold rush decoration mixed with 7/11 lighting), they don't take debit/credit cards, few choices on toppings,. Their yogurt is not bad, but it isn't unique in any way either.

Skip the lines and visit your closet yogurt</Review>
